 PARSE: inheres_in(attribute(n(mole)+n(fraction)),located_in(n(carbon)+n(dioxide),material(cls(http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/ENVO_00002005,air))))
 PARSE: located_in(inheres_in(attribute(n(mole)+n(fraction)),n(carbon)+n(dioxide)),material(cls(http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/ENVO_00002005,air)))
